Let's talk about common questions from creators when we do a payout.\n\nThe two biggest questions I get are:\n\n(1) I didn't get a payment\n(2) My payment was low\n\nOn (1), there is a minimum payout threshold of $10. If you don't meet the threshold, you aren't paid during that payout. You do of course keep accumulating earnings until you reach the threshold, until $10 is reached.\n\nThere are many practical reasons for this. The most important reason is fees associated with the transfer, which would potentially eat into a creator's earnings.\n\nOn (2), I've looked into dozens of cases about low payouts, especially for high follower / high impression accounts. Many creators assume that ads CPM x impression = their payout, but unfortunately it's not that simple. Although high impressions are of course correlated with a larger payout, the demographic of your audience and how they engage is also a very important factor.\n\nMajor factors that explain why such an account may receive a lower payout than expected include:\n\n1. Ads are shown, but the audience is not Verified. Revenue is only earned for ads shown to Verified users. This is one of many ways we mitigate attempts to manipulate the program.\n\n2. Ads are shown, but the ad spend on ads shown to the creator's demographic is low. It's a revenue share program - creators earn a % of what X earns. Ads generate more revenue in different markets and to different audiences.\n\n3. Some of the creator's content may not be suitable for ads. If we can't show ads on some of your posts, that affects your revenue.\n\n4. Content is compelling to scroll by in the timeline, but not compelling to reply to. Typically these accounts that generate high impressions but low replies - meaning less ads shown to their followers.\n\nEverything I covered here can also be seen in the terms of the Ad Revenue program here: https://t.co/eBU9zOH4h9\n\nWe'd like to improve the transparency in the product itself to help creators better understand how well their content is monetizing and what they can do to improve it.
